This module encapsulates everything required to reliably publish domain\n//! events to an external broker while guaranteeing atomic persistence of the\n//! associated business transaction (Transactional Outbox pattern).\n//!\n//! A high-level overview of the workflow:\n//!\n//! 1.  Business service saves its state changes inside a SQL transaction.\n//! 2.  The same transaction stores an `OutboxEvent` row\n//!     inside `event_outbox` (JSONB payload).\n//! 3.  The [`OutboxProcessor`] picks up un-published events in batches,\n//!     publishes them to NATS, and marks them as dispatched.\n//!\n//! The implementation is `async`/`await` based and leverages\n//! industry-grade crates such as `sqlx`, `async-nats`, and `tracing`.\n\nuse std::{fmt, time::Duration};\n\nuse async_nats::{jetstream, Client as NatsClient, ConnectOptions};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{de::DeserializeOwned, Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse sqlx::{PgPool, Postgres, Transaction};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::time::sleep;\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, instrument};\n\n/// The global NATS subject for EduPulse Live domain events.\n///\n/// Each microservice subscribes using its own durable consumer\n/// and optionally leverages JetStream for at-least-once delivery guarantees.\npub static NATS_SUBJECT: &str = \"edupulse.domain.events\";\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Domain Event abstraction\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Every domain event must implement this marker trait.\n///\n/// The trait bounds guarantee that all events are serialisable and debuggable,\n/// which enables structured logging & telemetry.\npub trait DomainEvent: Serialize + DeserializeOwned + fmt::Debug + Send + Sync {\n    /// A stable string identifier (e.g. `learning_pulse.created`).\n    fn event_type(&self) -> &'static str;\n    /// SemVer style event versioning (`\"1.0\"` by convention).\n    fn version(&self) -> &'static str;\n}\n\n/// Envelope for all outbound events.\n///\n/// It contains generic metadata required by consumers to perform\n/// deserialisation and correlation.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct EventEnvelope<E: DomainEvent> {\n    pub event_id: uuid::Uuid,\n    pub event_type: &'static str,\n    pub version: &'static str,\n    pub occurred_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub aggregate_id: uuid::Uuid,\n    pub payload: E,\n}\n\n/// Helper to wrap a concrete event instance.\npub fn wrap_event<E: DomainEvent>(\n    aggregate_id: uuid::Uuid,\n    payload: E,\n) -> EventEnvelope<E> {\n    EventEnvelope {\n        event_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4(),\n        event_type: payload.event_type(),\n        version: payload.version(),\n        occurred_at: Utc::now(),\n        aggregate_id,\n        payload,\n    }\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Outbox persistence\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Row inside `event_outbox` table.\n///\n/// Inserted within the same DB transaction as the originating command.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize, sqlx::FromRow)]\npub struct OutboxEvent {\n    pub id: i64,\n    pub aggregate_id: uuid::Uuid,\n    pub event_type: String,\n    pub version: String,\n    pub payload: serde_json::Value,\n    pub occurred_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub published_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n}\n\n/// Persist a new domain event in the outbox table.\n///\n/// Must be invoked within the caller's SQL transaction.\n#[instrument(skip(tx, envelope))]\npub async fn persist_event<E>(\n    tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n    envelope: &EventEnvelope<E>,\n) -> Result<(), OutboxError>\nwhere\n    E: DomainEvent,\n{\n    let payload_json = serde_json::to_value(&envelope.payload)?;\n    sqlx::query!(\n        r#\"\n        INSERT INTO event_outbox \n            (aggregate_id, event_type, version, payload, occurred_at)\n        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)\n        \"#,\n        envelope.aggregate_id,\n        envelope.event_type,\n        envelope.version,\n        payload_json,\n        envelope.occurred_at,\n    )\n    .execute(&mut *tx)\n    .await?;\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Outbox processor implementation\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Number of events we fetch per batch to reduce DB contention.\nconst BATCH_SIZE: i64 = 250;\n\n/// Processor error surface.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum OutboxError {\n    #[error(\"database error: {0}\")]\n    Db(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"serialization error: {0}\")]\n    Serde(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"NATS error: {0}\")]\n    Nats(#[from] async_nats::Error),\n}\n\n/// Background worker which iteratively drains the `event_outbox` table\n/// and forwards the events to NATS JetStream.\npub struct OutboxProcessor {\n    pg_pool: PgPool,\n    nats: jetstream::Context,\n}\n\nimpl OutboxProcessor {\n    /// Constructs a new [`OutboxProcessor`].\n    pub async fn new(pg_pool: PgPool, nats_url: &str) -> Result<Self, OutboxError> {\n        let nats_client = NatsClient::connect_with_options(\n            nats_url,\n            ConnectOptions::with_name(\"edupulse-outbox\"),\n        )\n        .await?;\n        let jetstream = jetstream::new(nats_client);\n\n        Ok(Self {\n            pg_pool,\n            nats: jetstream,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Starts the infinite polling loop until `shutdown` future resolves.\n    ///\n    /// Caller decides the sleep interval between attempts.\n    #[instrument(skip(self, shutdown), name = \"outbox.run\")]\n    pub async fn run_until_stopped(\n        &self,\n        poll_interval: Duration,\n        mut shutdown: tokio::sync::watch::Receiver<()>,\n    ) {\n        loop {\n            tokio::select! {\n                _ = shutdown.changed() => {\n                    info!(\"Outbox processor received shutdown signal \u2013 finishing current batch\");\n                    break;\n                }\n                _ = self.tick() => {}\n            }\n\n            sleep(poll_interval).await;\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Outbox processor terminated gracefully\");\n    }\n\n    /// Execute a single polling cycle.\n    #[instrument(skip(self))]\n    pub async fn tick(&self) {\n        match self.process_batch().await {\n            Ok(count) => {\n                if count > 0 {\n                    info!(count, \"outbox events dispatched\");\n                } else {\n                    debug!(\"no events to dispatch\");\n                }\n            }\n            Err(err) => {\n                error!(?err, \"failed to process outbox batch\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Fetch a batch of pending events, publish, and mark as dispatched.\n    #[instrument(skip(self), err)]\n    async fn process_batch(&self) -> Result<u64, OutboxError> {\n        let mut tx = self.pg_pool.begin().await?;\n\n        // Step 1: select for update \u2013 prevents concurrent processors\n        let events: Vec<OutboxEvent> = sqlx::query_as!(\n            OutboxEvent,\n            r#\"\n            SELECT * FROM event_outbox\n            WHERE published_at IS NULL\n            ORDER BY id\n            FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED\n            LIMIT $1\n            \"#,\n            BATCH_SIZE\n        )\n        .fetch_all(&mut tx)\n        .await?;\n\n        if events.is_empty() {\n            tx.rollback().await?;\n            return Ok(0);\n        }\n\n        // Step 2: publish each event to NATS\n        for evt in &events {\n            let payload_bytes = serde_json::to_vec(&evt)?;\n            self.nats\n                .publish(NATS_SUBJECT, payload_bytes.into())\n                .await?;\n        }\n\n        // Step 3: update published stamp\n        sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            UPDATE event_outbox\n            SET published_at = NOW()\n            WHERE id = ANY($1)\n            \"#,\n            &events.iter().map(|e| e.id).collect::<Vec<_>>()\n        )\n        .execute(&mut tx)\n        .await?;\n\n        tx.commit().await?;\n        Ok(events.len() as u64)\n    }\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Example domain event\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Fired when a new learning pulse (challenge) is created by a teacher.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct LearningPulseCreated {\n    pub pulse_id: uuid::Uuid,\n    pub author_id: uuid::Uuid,\n    pub title: String,\n    pub summary: String,\n}\n\nimpl DomainEvent for LearningPulseCreated {\n    fn event_type(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"learning_pulse.created\"\n    }\n\n    fn version(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"1.0\"\n    }\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Convenience API for application services\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Publish a newly generated domain event inside an existing SQL transaction.\n///\n/// Typical usage in a service command handler:\n///\n/// ```ignore\n/// let mut tx = pool.begin().await?;\n/// let envelope = wrap_event(aggregate_id, LearningPulseCreated { \u2026 });\n/// persist_event(&mut tx, &envelope).await?;\n/// tx.commit().await?;\n/// ```\npub async fn publish_domain_event<E>(\n    tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n    aggregate_id: uuid::Uuid,\n    event: E,\n) -> Result<(), OutboxError>\nwhere\n    E: DomainEvent,\n{\n    let envelope = wrap_event(aggregate_id, event);\n    persist_event(tx, &envelope).await\n}\n```",

This module wires domain events to asynchronous handlers while persisting\n//! them into an append-only event store.  Designed to live inside the core API\n//! crate, it exposes a minimal fa\u00e7ade so that higher-level modules\n//! Highlights\n//! ----------\n//! \u2022 Tokio-powered, back-pressure-aware broadcast channel  \n//! \u2022 Pluggable `EventStore` (in-memory + SQLx/Postgres ref. impl)  \n//! \u2022 Dynamic subscription registry using `async_trait` + `DashMap`  \n//! \u2022 JSON-serialised events for wire compatibility (RabbitMQ/NATS/etc.)  \n//! \u2022 Tracing-instrumented for observability\n//!\n//! QuizSubmitted {\n        quiz_id: Uuid,\n        student_id: Uuid,\n        score: u8,\n        submitted_at: UnixTimestamp,\n    },\n    // --- truncated: add more events as needed ---\n}\n\n/// Simple millisecond-precision unix timestamp wrapper.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct UnixTimestamp(u64);\n\nimpl Default for UnixTimestamp {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self(\n            SystemTime::now()\n                .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)\n                .expect(\"time went backwards\")\n                .as_millis() as u64,\n        )\n    }\n}\n\n/// Persistence fa\u00e7ade for storing domain events.\n///\n/// The event store is append-only and can be replayed for audits, projections\n/// or rebuilding read models.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait EventStore: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn append(&self, event: &DomainEvent) -> Result<()>;\n    async fn stream_all<E>(&self) -> Result<Vec<E>>\n    where\n        E: DeserializeOwned + Send + 'static;\n}\n\n/// In-memory reference implementation; suitable for tests / dev playground.\n#[derive(Debug, Default)]\npub struct InMemoryEventStore {\n    events: tokio::sync::RwLock<Vec<Vec<u8>>>,\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl EventStore for InMemoryEventStore {\n    #[instrument(skip(self, event))]\n    async fn append(&self, }\n    }\n\n    /// Emit a single event.\n    #[instrument(skip(self))]\n    pub async fn emit(&self, evt: DomainEvent) -> Result<()> {\n        self.store.append(&evt).await?;\n        self.tx\n            .send(evt)\n            .map_err(|e| anyhow::anyhow!(\"broadcast failure: {e}\"))?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Register a handler; idempotent per handler name.\n    pub fn register_handler<H>(&self, handler: H)\n    where\n        H: EventHandler,\n    {\n        if self.handlers.insert(handler.name(), Box::new(handler)).is_some() {\n            warn!(\"handler {} replaced at runtime\", handler.name());\n        } else {\n            info!(\"handler {} registered\", handler.name());\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Spawn a worker pool that fans-out events to handlers.\n    ///\n    /// Each worker owns an mpsc channel (to avoid contention) and reads from\n    /// the *same* broadcast channel.  This guarantees at-least-once delivery to\n    /// each handler.\n    pub fn start_worker_pool(self: &Arc<Self>, workers: usize) -> Vec<JoinHandle<()>> {\n        let mut handles = Vec::with_capacity(workers);\n        for id in 0..workers {\n            let (tx, mut rx) = mpsc::channel::<DomainEvent>(CHANNEL_CAPACITY);\n            self.worker_txs.push(tx);\n\n            let bus = Arc::clone(self);\n            let mut broadcast_rx = bus.tx.subscribe();\n            handles.push(spawn(async move {\n                info!(worker = id, \"event worker started\");\n                loop {\n                    select! {\n                        Ok(evt) = broadcast_rx.recv() => {\n                            // fan-in to single queue\n                            if let Err(e) = rx.try_send(evt) {\n                                debug!(%e, worker = id, \"worker queue full; dropping\");\n                            }\n                        },\n\n                        Some(evt) = rx.recv() => {\n                            for item in bus.handlers.iter() {\n                                let handler = item.value();\n                                let evt_clone = evt.clone();\n                                let h_name = handler.name();\n                                let res = handler.handle(evt_clone).await;\n                                if let Err(e) = res {\n                                    error!(%e, handler = h_name, \"event handler failed\");\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }));\n        }\n        handles\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/* ----------------------- Example Production Handler ----------------------- */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Tantivy-powered search indexer.\n///\n/// In a real deployment this would:\n/// 1. Dependencies (Cargo.toml excerpt):\n//! ----------------------------------\n//! async-nats = { version = \"0.33\", default-features = false, features = [\"tls\"] }\n//! sqlx       = { version = \"0.7\", features = [\"runtime-tokio-native-tls\", \"postgres\", \"json\"] }\n//! serde      = { version = \"1.0\", features = [\"derive\"] }\n//! serde_json = \"1.0\"\n//! thiserror  = \"1.0\"\n//! uuid       = { version = \"1.3\", features = [\"v4\", \"serde\"] }\n//! chrono     = { version = \"0.4\", features = [\"serde\"] }\n//! tracing    = \"0.1\"\n//! futures    = \"0.3\"\n//! anyhow     = \"1.0\"\n//! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nuse std::sync::Arc;\n\nuse async_nats::{Client as NatsClient, PublishAck};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse futures::{Stream, StreamExt, TryStreamExt};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse sqlx::{postgres::PgPoolOptions, PgPool, Postgres, Transaction};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tracing::{instrument, span, Level};\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\n/// Type alias for the *canonical* aggregate identifier.\n/// (We keep it generic enough to be shared among all contexts.)\npub type AggregateId = Uuid;\n\n/// A type-safe identifier used for exactly-once message guarantees.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct EventId(Uuid);\n\nimpl Default for EventId {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        EventId(Uuid::new_v4())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Core domain events.\n///\n/// NOTE: In a real system this enum would live in its own crate and be shared\n/// through the workspace. default.\npub type Result<T, E = EventError> = std::result::Result<T, E>;\n\n/// Data-access abstraction for the event store.\n///\n/// Implementation uses *optimistic concurrency control* (OCC) via a `seq`\n/// column coupled with a *partial unique index* on (`aggregate_id`, `seq`).\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct EventStore {\n    pool: Arc<PgPool>,\n}\n\nimpl EventStore {\n    pub async fn connect(database_url: &str, max_connections: u32) -> Result<Self> {\n        let pool = PgPoolOptions::new()\n            .max_connections(max_connections)\n            .after_connect(|mut conn, _meta| {\n                Box::pin(async move {\n                    // Force UTC timezone for timestamp determinism.\n                    sqlx::query(\"SET TIME ZONE 'UTC'\").execute(&mut conn).await?;\n                    Ok(())\n                })\n            })\n            .connect(database_url)\n            .await?;\n\n        Ok(Self {\n            pool: Arc::new(pool),\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Append a *single* event to the store with OCC.\n    ///\n    /// Returns the stored [`EventEnvelope`] (with auto-generated id + timestamp).\n    #[instrument(skip(self, tx))]\n    pub async fn append_one(\n        &self,\n        mut tx: Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n        aggregate_id: AggregateId,\n        expected_seq: i64,\n        event: DomainEvent,\n        correlation_id: Option<EventId>,\n    ) -> Result<EventEnvelope> {\n        // Next sequence number we intend to store.\n        let next_seq = expected_seq + 1;\n\n        let envelope = EventEnvelope::new(aggregate_id, next_seq, event, correlation_id);\n        let serialized = serde_json::to_value(&envelope)?;\n\n        let res = sqlx::query(\n            r#\"\n            INSERT INTO event_store (id, aggregate_id, seq, payload)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4)\n            ON CONFLICT (aggregate_id, seq) DO NOTHING\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .bind(envelope.id.0)\n        .bind(envelope.aggregate_id)\n        .bind(envelope.seq)\n        .bind(&serialized)\n        .execute(&mut *tx)\n        .await?;\n\n        if res.rows_affected() == 0 {\n            // Sequence already taken \u2013 someone else wrote concurrently.\n            let actual = self\n                .latest_sequence_for(&aggregate_id)\n                .await?\n                .unwrap_or_default();\n\n            return Err(EventError::Concurrency {\n                aggregate_id,\n                expected: expected_seq,\n                actual,\n            });\n        }\n\n        Ok(envelope)\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the *last* known sequence for an aggregate.  If absent, returns\n    /// `None`.\n    #[instrument(skip(self))]\n    pub async fn latest_sequence_for(&self, aggregate_id: &AggregateId) -> Result<Option<i64>> {\n        let seq = sqlx::query_scalar::<_, Option<i64>>(\n            r#\"\n            SELECT seq\n            FROM event_store\n            WHERE aggregate_id = $1\n            ORDER BY seq DESC\n            LIMIT 1\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .bind(aggregate_id)\n        .fetch_one(&*self.pool)\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(seq)\n    }\n\n    /// Open an *unbounded* stream for the whole event log.\n    /// Clients should apply their own back-pressure strategies.\n    #[instrument(skip(self))]\n    pub fn stream_all(&self) -> impl Stream<Item = Result<EventEnvelope>> + '_ {\n        sqlx::query_scalar::<_, serde_json::Value>(\n            r#\"SELECT payload FROM event_store ORDER BY id\"#,\n        )\n        .fetch(&*self.pool)\n        .map_ok(|val| serde_json::from_value::<EventEnvelope>(val))\n        .try_buffered(64) // concurrent JSON deserialization\n    }\n\n    /// Helper to begin a transaction.\n    pub async fn begin(&self) -> Result<Transaction<'_, Postgres>> {\n        Ok(self.pool.begin().await?)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Publishes events to NATS with at-least-once semantics.\n///\n/// It is intentionally *thin*: we keep transport concerns outside domain\n/// services.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct EventPublisher {\n    nats: NatsClient,\n    subject_prefix: Arc<str>,\n}\n\nimpl EventPublisher {\n    pub async fn connect(nats_url: &str, subject_prefix: impl AsRef<str>) -> Result<Self> {\n        // TLS enabled by default (async_nats w/ `tls` feature).\n        let nats = async_nats::connect(nats_url).await?;\n\n        Ok(Self {\n            nats,\n            subject_prefix: Arc::from(subject_prefix.as_ref()),\n        })\n    }\n\n    fn subject_for(&self, event: &DomainEvent) -> String {\n        // Use enum variant name as the subject suffix.\n        let variant = match event {\n            DomainEvent::LessonPublished { .. } => \"LessonPublished\",\n            DomainEvent::QuizSubmitted { .. } => \"QuizSubmitted\",\n            DomainEvent::BadgeAwarded { .. } => \"BadgeAwarded\",\n            DomainEvent::PaymentProcessed { .. } => \"PaymentProcessed\",\n        };\n        format!(\"{}.{}\", self.subject_prefix, variant)\n    }\n\n    /// Publish an envelope to NATS.  Returns the `PublishAck`.\n    #[instrument(skip(self, envelope))]\n    pub async fn publish(&self, envelope: &EventEnvelope) -> Result<PublishAck> {\n        let subject = self.subject_for(&envelope.event);\n        let payload = serde_json::to_vec(envelope)?;\n\n        Ok(self.nats.publish(subject, payload.into()).await?)\n    }\n}\n\n/// High-level facade combining EventContext {\n    store: EventStore,\n    publisher: EventPublisher,\n}\n\nimpl EventContext {\n    pub fn new(store: EventStore, publisher: EventPublisher) -> Self {\n        Self { store, publisher }\n    }\n\n    /// Wrap a *business* operation in a transaction and publish all newly\n    /// appended events atomically (two-phase commit).\n    #[instrument(skip(self, op))]\n    pub async fn commit<F, Fut, T>(&self, op: F) -> Result<T>\n    where\n        F: FnOnce(&Self, &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>) -> Fut + Send + Sync,\n        Fut: std::future::Future<Output = Result<T>> + Send,\n        T: Send,\n    {\n        let mut tx = self.store.begin().await?;\n\n        let result = op(self, &mut tx).await?;\n\n        // Extract fresh events written within the tx:\n        let staged_events: Vec<EventEnvelope> = sqlx::query_scalar(\n            r#\"\n            SELECT payload\n            FROM event_store\n            WHERE transaction_timestamp() - statement_timestamp() < INTERVAL '1 second'\n              AND txid_current() = txid_current()\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .fetch_all(&mut *tx)\n        .await?\n        .into_iter()\n        .map(|val: serde_json::Value| serde_json::from_value(val))\n        .collect::<std::result::Result<_, _>>()?;\n\n        // Commit DB first (outbox pattern).\n        tx.commit().await?;\n\n        // Publish *after* commit to avoid phantom events.\n        for env in staged_events {\n            // We could `spawn` but prefer sequential to simplify ordering/acks.\n            self.publisher.publish(&env).await?;\n        }\n\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    /// Convenience wrapper: append + publish inside a running tx.\n    #[instrument(skip(self, tx))]\n    pub async fn append(\n        &self,\n        tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n        aggregate_id: AggregateId,\n        expected_seq: i64,\n        event: DomainEvent,\n        correlation_id: Option<EventId>,\n    ) -> Result<EventEnvelope> {\n        let env = self\n            .store\n            .append_one(\n                tx.as_mut(),\n                aggregate_id,\n                expected_seq,\n                event,\n                correlation_id,\n            )\n            .await?;\n\n        // Buffer the event in the transaction\u2019s local temp table for later pickup.\n        sqlx::query(\n            r#\"\n            INSERT INTO _staged_events (payload) VALUES ($1)\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .bind(sqlx::types::Json(&env))\n        .execute(&mut *tx)\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(env)\n    }\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Database bootstrap helpers (run via (e.g., refinery, sqlx-migrate).\npub async fn bootstrap_event_schema(pool: &PgPool) -> anyhow::Result<()> {\n    let mut conn = pool.acquire().await?;\n\n    // Use idempotent `IF NOT EXISTS` to keep it re-runnable.\n    sqlx::query(\n        r#\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS event_store (\n            id            UUID            PRIMARY KEY,\n            aggregate_id  UUID            NOT NULL,\n            seq           BIGINT          NOT NULL,\n            payload       JSONB           NOT NULL,\n\n            CONSTRAINT seq_unique UNIQUE (aggregate_id, seq)\n        );\n\n        -- Fast lookup for aggregates\n        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_event_store_aggregate\n            ON event_store (aggregate_id);\n\n        -- Staging area for outbox pattern (tx-scoped)\n This module demonstrates a pragmatic implementation of the\n//!  \u2022 domain\u2010event pattern,\n//!  \u2022 transactional outbox,\n//!  \u2022 asynchronous relay into a broker (e.g. NATS, Rabbit, Kafka),\n//! while keeping the core API synchronous and highly responsive.\n//\n//! The implementation follows EduPulse\u2019s architecture guidelines: Service\n//! layer + Repository pattern, backed by a PostgreSQL database via `sqlx`.\n//!\n//! NOTE: In a real workspace this file would live under `src/infra/\u2026`, but the\n//!       challenge requires the path `src/module_77.txt`.  The extension is left\n//!       unchanged for demonstration purposes, yet `cargo` happily compiles it\n//!       because Rust only considers the `mod` system, not the filename suffix.\n\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse futures::{stream::FuturesUnordered, StreamExt};\nuse serde::{de::DeserializeOwned, Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse sqlx::{postgres::PgRow, query, query_as, PgPool, Postgres, Row, Transaction};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::{\n    select,\n    sync::mpsc::{self, Receiver, Sender},\n    task::JoinHandle,\n    time,\n};\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, instrument, warn};\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\nconst MAX_RETRY_COUNT: i16 = 5;\nconst BATCH_SIZE: i64 = 100;\n\n/// High-level domain events used throughout EduPulse.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(tag = \"type\", content = \"data\")]\npub enum DomainEvent {\n    /// A new learning pulse was published by an instructor.\n    PulseCreated {\n        pulse_id: Uuid,\n        author_id: Uuid,\n        title: String,\n        published_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    },\n\n    /// A learner submitted an answer to a pulse.\n    PulseAnswered {\n        pulse_id: Uuid,\n        answer_id: Uuid,\n        student_id: Uuid,\n        answered_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    },\n\n    /// A badge has been awarded.\n    BadgeAwarded {\n        badge_id: Uuid,\n        user_id: Uuid,\n        reason: String,\n        awarded_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Envelope that wraps any [`DomainEvent`] together with outbox metadata.\n///\n/// This allows fault-tolerant, ordered replay while keeping the event payload\n/// opaque to the infrastructure layer.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct EventEnvelope {\n    pub id: Uuid,\n    pub aggregate_id: Uuid,\n    pub occurred_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub event: DomainEvent,\n}\n\n/// Database representation of an outbox message.\n///\n/// The table is expected to look like:\n///\n/// ```sql\n/// CREATE TABLE outbox (\n///     id              uuid      PRIMARY KEY,\n///     aggregate_id    uuid      NOT NULL,\n///     event_type      text      NOT NULL,\n///     payload         jsonb     NOT NULL,\n///     occurred_at     timestamptz NOT NULL,\n///     retries         smallint     NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n///     locked_until    timestamptz,\n///     delivered_at    timestamptz\n/// );\n/// CREATE INDEX idx_outbox_retries ON outbox (retries);\n/// CREATE INDEX idx_outbox_pending ON outbox (delivered_at) WHERE delivered_at IS NULL;\n/// ```\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\nstruct OutboxRow {\n    id: Uuid,\n    aggregate_id: Uuid,\n    event_type: String,\n    payload: serde_json::Value,\n    occurred_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    retries: i16,\n}\n\nimpl OutboxRow {\n    #[instrument(level = \"trace\", skip_all)]\n    fn from_envelope(envelope: EventEnvelope) -> sqlx::Result<Self> {\n        let event_type = match &envelope.event {\n            DomainEvent::PulseCreated { .. } => \"PulseCreated\",\n            DomainEvent::PulseAnswered { .. } => \"PulseAnswered\",\n            DomainEvent::BadgeAwarded { .. } => \"BadgeAwarded\",\n        }\n        .to_string();\n\n        Ok(Self {\n            id: envelope.id,\n            aggregate_id: envelope.aggregate_id,\n            event_type,\n            payload: serde_json::to_value(&envelope.event)?,\n            occurred_at: envelope.occurred_at,\n            retries: 0,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Errors originating in the outbox layer.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum OutboxError {\n    #[error(\"Persistence failure: {0}\")]\n    Persistence(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"Serialization failure: {0}\")]\n    Serialization(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"Channel closed\")]\n    ChannelClosed,\n}\n\n/// Abstraction over anything that can store events in the outbox.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait OutboxRepository {\n    async fn save(\n        &self,\n        tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n        envelope: EventEnvelope,\n    ) -> Result<(), OutboxError>;\n}\n\n/// PostgreSQL implementation of the outbox repository.\npub struct PgOutboxRepository {\n    pool: PgPool,\n}\n\nimpl PgOutboxRepository {\n    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {\n        Self { pool }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl OutboxRepository for PgOutboxRepository {\n    #[instrument(level = \"debug\", skip_all, fields(event_id=%envelope.id))]\n    async fn save(\n        &self,\n        tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n        envelope: EventEnvelope,\n    ) -> Result<(), OutboxError> {\n        let row = OutboxRow::from_envelope(envelope)?;\n        query!(\n            r#\"\n row.event_type,\n            row.payload,\n            row.occurred_at,\n        )\n        .execute(&mut *tx)\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Contract for anything that can publish events from the outbox to an external\n/// broker (NATS, RabbitMQ, Kafka, \u2026).\n#[async_trait]\npub trait EventPublisher {\n    async fn publish(&self, envelope: EventEnvelope) -> Result<(), anyhow::Error>;\n}\n\n/// =============================================================================================\n/// Background task that continuously pulls pending messages, publishes them,\n/// and marks them as delivered (or retries with exponential back-off).\n/// =============================================================================================\npub struct OutboxRelay<P> {\n    pool: PgPool,\n    publisher: P,\n    interval: Duration,\n    concurrency: usize,\n}\n\nimpl<P> OutboxRelay<P>\nwhere\n    P: EventPublisher + Send + Sync + 'static,\n{\n    pub fn new(pool: PgPool, publisher: P) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            pool,\n            publisher,\n            interval: Duration::from_secs(5),\n            concurrency: 8,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn with_interval(mut self, duration: Duration) -> Self {\n        self.interval = duration;\n        self\n    }\n\n    pub fn with_concurrency(mut self, n: usize) -> Self {\n        self.concurrency = n;\n        self\n    }\n\n    /// Spawns the relay as an independent Tokio task and returns the join handle.\n    pub fn spawn(self) -> JoinHandle<()> {\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            self.run().await;\n        })\n    }\n\n    #[instrument(name = \"outbox_relay\", skip(self))]\n    pub async fn run(self) {\n        info!(\"OutboxRelay started; interval = {:?}\", self.interval);\n\n        let (tx, rx) = mpsc::channel::<EventEnvelope>(self.concurrency * 2);\n\n        // Spawn worker tasks\n        let mut workers: FuturesUnordered<_> = (0..self.concurrency)\n            .map(|idx| {\n                let rx = rx.clone();\n                let publisher = &self.publisher;\n                tokio::spawn(worker_task(idx, rx, publisher))\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        drop(rx); // allow graceful exit when all senders are dropped\n\n        let mut ticker = time::interval(self.interval);\n\n        loop {\n            select! {\n                _ = ticker.tick() => {\n                    match self.fetch_pending(&tx).await {\n                        Ok(count) => {\n                            debug!(%count, \"Fetched pending events\");\n                        }\n                        Err(e) => {\n                            error!(error = ?e, \"Failed to fetch pending events\");\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n\n                // Drain finished workers to avoid memory leak of JoinHandles.\n                Some(res) = workers.next() => {\n                    if let Err(e) = res {\n                        error!(error = ?e, \"Worker crashed\");\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Fetches pending events and sends them to the worker channel.\n    #[instrument(skip_all, fields(batch_size = BATCH_SIZE))]\n    async fn fetch_pending(&self, tx_chan: &Sender<EventEnvelope>) -> Result<usize, OutboxError> {\n        let mut conn = self.pool.acquire().await?;\n\n        // Lock rows to prevent double delivery from multiple nodes.\n        let rows: Vec<PgRow> = query(\n            r#\"\n            UPDATE outbox\n            SET locked_until = NOW() + INTERVAL '1 minute'\n            WHERE id IN (\n                SELECT id\n                FROM outbox\n                WHERE delivered_at IS NULL\n                  AND (locked_until IS NULL OR locked_until < NOW())\n                  AND retries < $1\n                ORDER BY occurred_at\n                LIMIT $2\n                FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED\n            )\n            RETURNING id, aggregate_id, event_type, payload, occurred_at, retries\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .bind(MAX_RETRY_COUNT)\n        .bind(BATCH_SIZE)\n        .fetch_all(&mut *conn)\n        .await?;\n\n        let count = rows.len();\n\n        for row in rows {\n            let envelope = EventEnvelope {\n                id: row.get(\"id\"),\n                aggregate_id: row.get(\"aggregate_id\"),\n                occurred_at: row.get(\"occurred_at\"),\n                event: serde_json::from_value::<DomainEvent>(row.get(\"payload\"))?,\n            };\n\n            tx_chan.send(envelope).await.map_err(|_| OutboxError::ChannelClosed)?;\n        }\n\n        Ok(count)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Background worker that receives envelopes and publishes them through the\n/// provided `EventPublisher`.\n#[instrument(skip(rx, publisher))]\nasync fn worker_task<P>(idx: usize, mut rx: Receiver<EventEnvelope>, publisher: &P)\nwhere\n    P: EventPublisher + Send + Sync + 'static,\n{\n    while let Some(envelope) = rx.recv().await {\n        match publisher.publish(envelope.clone()).await {\n            Ok(()) => {\n                debug!(worker = idx, event_id = %envelope.id, \"Published event\");\n                // Mark as delivered\n                // We perform a fire-and-forget update; eventual consistency is enough here.\n                if let Err(e) = mark_delivered(envelope.id).await {\n                    warn!(error=?e, \"Failed to mark outbox row as delivered\");\n                }\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                error!(worker = idx, event_id = %envelope.id, error = ?e, \"Failed to publish event\");\n                if let Err(db_err) = increment_retries(envelope.id).await {\n                    error!(error = ?db_err, \"Failed to increment retry counter\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Updates `delivered_at` timestamp.\nasync fn mark_delivered(event_id: Uuid) -> sqlx::Result<()> {\n    // Acquire from a global PgPool. In a real project we\u2019d inject it, but for\n    // this isolated file we rely on the `DATABASE_URL` environment variable and\n    // lazy connection init.\n    static POOL: once_cell::sync::Lazy<PgPool> = once_cell::sync::Lazy::new(|| {\n        let rt = tokio::runtime::Runtime::new().expect(\"tokio rt\");\n        rt.block_on(async {\n            let url = std::env::var(\"DATABASE_URL\")\n                .expect(\"DATABASE_URL must be set for outbox relay\");\n            PgPool::connect(&url).await.expect(\"failed to connect\")\n        })\n    });\n\n    query!(\n        \"UPDATE outbox SET delivered_at = NOW() WHERE id = $1\",\n        event_id\n    )\n    .execute(&*POOL)\n    .await?;\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Increments retry counter for failed deliveries.\nasync fn increment_retries(event_id: Uuid) -> sqlx::Result<()> {\n    static POOL: once_cell::sync::Lazy<PgPool> = once_cell::sync::Lazy::new(|| {\n        let rt = tokio::runtime::Runtime::new().expect(\"tokio rt\");\n        rt.block_on(async {\n            let url = std::env::var(\"DATABASE_URL\")\n                .expect(\"DATABASE_URL must be set for outbox relay\");\n            PgPool::connect(&url).await.expect(\"failed to connect\")\n        })\n    });\n\n    query!(\n        \"UPDATE outbox SET retries = retries + 1 WHERE id = $1\",\n        event_id\n    )\n    .execute(&*POOL)\n    .await?;\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// =============================================================================================\n/// Mock publisher for {\n        // Serialize the event to JSON to keep schema flexible.\n        let payload = serde_json::to_string(evt)\n            .map_err(|e| redis::RedisError::from((redis::ErrorKind::TypeError, e.to_string())))?;\n        let mut conn = self.client.get_async_connection().await?;\n        conn.publish::<&str, String, ()>(&self.channel, payload).await?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n// {\n    type Error = Error;\n    type Future = Ready<Result<Self, Self::Error>>;\n\n    fn from_request(req: &ServiceRequest, _payload: &mut actix_http::Payload) -> Self::Future {\n        // Read `Authorization: Bearer ...` header and verify JWT. In a\n        // production system you would cache decoding keys and handle\n        // algorithm negotiation.\n        let auth_hdr = req\n            .headers()\n            .get(header::AUTHORIZATION)\n            .and_then(|h| h.to_str().ok())\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        if !auth_hdr.starts_with(\"Bearer \") {\n            error!(\"Missing bearer token\");\n            return ready(Err(ServiceError::Unauthorized.into()));\n        }\n\n        let token = &auth_hdr[7..];\n        let key = jwt::DecodingKey::from_secret(b\"super-secret-change-me\"); // TODO: rotate\n        let validation = jwt::Validation::new(JWT_ALGO);\n\n        match jwt::decode::<Claims>(token, &key, &validation) {\n            Ok(data) => ready(Ok(AuthenticatedUser(data.claims.sub))),\n            Err(err) => {\n                error!(\"JWT validation error: {:?}\", err);\n                ready(Err(ServiceError::Unauthorized.into()))\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ======================================================================\n//                       HTTP Request / Response DTOs\n// ======================================================================\n\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct SubmitResponseReq {\n    pulse_id: Uuid,\n    body: \"postgres://edupulse:edupulse@localhost:5432/edupulse\".to_string()\n    });\n    let redis_url = std::env::var(\"REDIS_URL\")\n        .unwrap_or_else(|_| \"redis://127.0.0.1:6379/\".into());\n Arc::new(RedisPublisher::new(redis_client.clone())) as Arc<dyn EventPublisher>;\n\n    let learning_pulse_service = LearningPulseService::new(pg_pool.clone(), publisher);\n\n    // Redis session store .expect(\"failed to create redis session store\");\n\n    info!(\"Starting HTTPS server at {}\", bind_addr);\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Build This module provides a production-ready* implementation of the\n//! Outbox/Inbox pattern for EduPulse Live.  All domain events are first\n//! persisted inside the same Postgres transaction that modified the\n//! aggregate and are later *atomically* published to the message broker\n//! (e.g. RabbitMQ).  This guarantees *at-least-once* delivery without\n//! sacrificing database consistency.\n//!\n//! # Architecture\n//! 1. Domain layer inserts a row into the `outbox_events` table\n//!    through [`OutboxRepository::insert`].\n//! 2. [`OutboxProcessor`] polls the table on an interval (or is triggered\n//!    by NOTIFY/LISTEN) and publishes unpublished events.\n//! 3. After a successful publish it marks the event as `published_at`.\n//!\n//! # Usage\n//! ```no_run\n//! #[tokio::main]\n//! async fn main() -> anyhow::Result<()> {\n//!     env_logger::init();\n//!\n//!     let db = PgPoolOptions::new()\n//!         .max_connections(5)\n//!         .connect(\"postgres://user:password@localhost/edupulse\")\n//!         .await?;\n//!\n//!     // Initialise AMQP connection\n//!     let amqp_addr = \"amqp://guest:guest@127.0.0.1:5672/%2f\";\n//!     let publisher = RabbitMqPublisher::connect(amqp_addr, \"edupulse.events\").await?;\n//!\n//!     // Fire-and-forget background processing task\n//!     OutboxProcessor::spawn(db.clone(), publisher);\n//!\n//!     // \u2026 start REST API, etc.\n//!     Ok(())\n//! }\n//! ```\n//! *Error handling, retries, and back-off have been implemented but can be\n//! expanded with metrics, dead-letter queues, etc.*\n\nuse std::sync::Arc;\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse backoff::{future::retry, ExponentialBackoff};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse lapin::{\n    options::{BasicPublishOptions, QueueDeclareOptions},\n    types::FieldTable,\n    BasicProperties, Channel, Connection, ConnectionProperties,\n};\nuse log::{error, info, warn};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse sqlx::{postgres::PgRow, PgPool, Row};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::{\n    sync::Mutex,\n    task::{self, JoinHandle},\n    time,\n};\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                Domain Event                                */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// A single row inside the `outbox_events` table.\n///\n/// NOTE: `payload` is stored as **raw JSON** to keep the table generic and\n/// future-proof.  Consumers can decode it based on the `event_type`.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize, Clone)]\npub struct OutboxEvent {\n    pub id: Uuid,\n    pub aggregate_type: String,\n    pub aggregate_id: Uuid,\n    pub event_type: String,\n    pub payload: serde_json::Value,\n    pub occurred_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub published_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                  Errors                                    */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Error, Debug)]\npub enum OutboxError {\n    #[error(\"database error: {0}\")]\n    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"AMQP error: {0}\")]\n    Amqp(#[from] lapin::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"serialization error: {0}\")]\n    Serde(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           Outbox Repository (DAO)                          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Repository responsible for accessing the `outbox_events` table.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct OutboxRepository {\n    pool: PgPool,\n}\n\nimpl OutboxRepository {\n    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {\n        Self { pool }\n    }\n\n    /// Inserts a new [`OutboxEvent`] within an existing transaction or\n    /// standalone if `tx` is `None`.\n    pub async fn insert(\n        &self,\n        mut event: OutboxEvent,\n        tx: Option<&mut sqlx::Transaction<'_, sqlx::Postgres>>,\n    ) -> Result<OutboxEvent, OutboxError> {\n        event.id = event.id; // ensure id exists\n        let query = sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            INSERT INTO outbox_events (\n                id,\n                aggregate_type,\n                aggregate_id,\n                event_type,\n                payload,\n                occurred_at,\n                published_at\n            ) VALUES ($1,$2,$3,$4,$5,$6,$7)\n            \"#,\n            event.id,\n            event.aggregate_type,\n            event.aggregate_id,\n            event.event_type,\n            event.payload,\n            event.occurred_at,\n            event.published_at\n        );\n\n        match tx {\n            Some(tx_ref) => {\n                query.execute(&mut *tx_ref).await?;\n            }\n            None => {\n                query.execute(&self.pool).await?;\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(event)\n    }\n\n    /// Fetches a batch of unpublished events, ordered by `occurred_at`.\n    pub async fn fetch_unpublished(\n        &self,\n        limit: i64,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<OutboxEvent>, OutboxError> {\n        let rows = sqlx::query(\n            r#\"\n            SELECT\n                id,\n                aggregate_type,\n                aggregate_id,\n                event_type,\n                payload,\n                occurred_at,\n                published_at\n            FROM outbox_events\n            WHERE published_at IS NULL\n            ORDER BY occurred_at\n            LIMIT $1\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .bind(limit)\n        .map(|row: PgRow| OutboxEvent {\n            id: row.get(\"id\"),\n            aggregate_type: row.get(\"aggregate_type\"),\n            aggregate_id: row.get(\"aggregate_id\"),\n            event_type: row.get(\"event_type\"),\n            payload: row.get::<serde_json::Value, _>(\"payload\"),\n            occurred_at: row.get(\"occurred_at\"),\n            published_at: row.get(\"published_at\"),\n        })\n        .fetch_all(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(rows)\n    }\n\n    /// Marks the event as published.\n    pub async fn mark_as_published(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<(), OutboxError> {\n        sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            UPDATE outbox_events\n            SET published_at = NOW()\n            WHERE id = $1\n            \"#,\n            id\n        )\n        .execute(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                             Event Publisher                                */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Trait that abstracts away the underlying message broker implementation.\n/// This allows swapping RabbitMQ for NATS, Kafka, etc. without touching the\n/// domain/application layer.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait EventPublisher: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn publish(&self, event: &OutboxEvent) -> Result<(), OutboxError>;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                             RabbitMQ Publisher                             */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Thin wrapper around a RabbitMQ channel that implements [`EventPublisher`].\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct RabbitMqPublisher {\n    channel: Arc<Channel>,\n    exchange: String,\n}\n\nimpl RabbitMqPublisher {\n    /// Establishes a connection and ensures that the declared exchange exists.\n    pub async fn connect(\n        amqp_addr: &str,\n        exchange: &str,\n    ) -> Result<Self, OutboxError> {\n        let conn = Connection::connect(amqp_addr, ConnectionProperties::default()).await?;\n        let channel = conn.create_channel().await?;\n\n        channel\n            .queue_declare(\n                exchange,\n                QueueDeclareOptions::default(),\n                FieldTable::default(),\n            )\n            .await?;\n\n        Ok(Self {\n            channel: Arc::new(channel),\n            exchange: exchange.to_string(),\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl EventPublisher for RabbitMqPublisher {\n    async fn publish(&self, event: &OutboxEvent) -> Result<(), OutboxError> {\n        let payload = serde_json::to_vec(event)?;\n        self.channel\n            .basic_publish(\n                \"\",\n                &self.exchange,\n                BasicPublishOptions::default(),\n                &payload,\n                BasicProperties::default()\n                    .with_content_type(\"application/json\".into())\n                    .with_message_id(event.id.to_string().into())\n                    .with_type(event.event_type.clone().into()),\n            )\n            .await?\n            .await?; // wait for broker confirmation\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                            Outbox Processor                                */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Responsible for periodically polling the DB, publishing events and\n/// updating their status. It runs indefinitely in a tokio task.\npub struct OutboxProcessor {\n    handle: JoinHandle<()>,\n}\n\nimpl OutboxProcessor {\n    /// Spawns the background `OutboxProcessor` task with sensible defaults.\n    ///\n    /// `poll_interval` defaults to 500 ms and `batch_size` to 100.\n    pub fn spawn<P>(pool: PgPool, publisher: P) -> Self\n    where\n        P: EventPublisher,\n    {\n        let poll_interval = Duration::from_millis(500);\n        let batch_size = 100;\n\n        let repo = OutboxRepository::new(pool);\n        let publisher = Arc::new(publisher);\n\n        let handle = task::spawn(async move {\n            let mut interval = time::interval(poll_interval);\n            loop {\n                interval.tick().await;\n                if let Err(err) =\n                    Self::drain_batch(&repo, Arc::clone(&publisher), batch_size).await\n                {\n                    error!(\"Error draining outbox: {:?}\", err);\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        Self { handle }\n    }\n\n    async fn drain_batch<P>(\n        repo: &OutboxRepository,\n        publisher: Arc<P>,\n        batch_size: i64,\n    ) -> Result<(), OutboxError>\n    where\n        P: EventPublisher,\n    {\n        // Fetch a batch; early return if empty\n        let events = repo.fetch_unpublished(batch_size).await?;\n        if events.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n\n        // Publish events sequentially (could be parallel with `join_all` if\n        // ordering isn't important)\n        for event in events {\n            let op = || async {\n                publisher.publish(&event).await?;\n                repo.mark_as_published(event.id).await?;\n                Ok::<(), OutboxError>(())\n            };\n\n            // Retry with exponential back-off (max ~10 min)\n            let mut backoff = ExponentialBackoff {\n                initial_interval: Duration::from_millis(250),\n                multiplier: 2.0,\n                max_interval: Duration::from_secs(30),\n                max_elapsed_time: Some(Duration::from_secs(600)),\n                ..Default::default()\n            };\n\n            if let Err(err) = retry(backoff, op).await {\n                // This should rarely happen; send to Sentry, Dead-letter, etc.\n                warn!(\"Failed to publish event {}: {:?}\", event.id, err);\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Waits for the background task to finish (e.g. on graceful shutdown).\n    pub async fn join(self) -> Result<(), task::JoinError> {\n        self.handle.await\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                   Tests                                    */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use sqlx::Executor;\n    use tokio::sync::Mutex;\n\n    /// Dummy in-memory publisher that records the number of published events.\n    #[derive(Default, Clone)]\n    struct MockPublisher {\n        published: Arc<Mutex<u32>>,\n    }\n\n    #[async_trait]\n    impl EventPublisher for MockPublisher {\n        async fn publish(&self, _event: &OutboxEvent) -> Result<(), OutboxError> {\n            let mut guard = self.published.lock().await;\n            *guard += 1;\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[sqlx::test(migrations = \"../migrations\")]\n    async fn processor_publishes_and_marks_event(pool: PgPool) -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>>\n    {\n        // Arrange\n        let repo = OutboxRepository::new(pool.clone());\n        let publisher = MockPublisher::default();\n        let now = Utc::now();\n\n        let event = OutboxEvent {\n            id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n            aggregate_type: \"Lesson\".into(),\n            aggregate_id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n            event_type: \"LessonPublished\".into(),\n            payload: serde_json::json!({\"title\": \"Intro\"}),\n            occurred_at: now,\n            published_at: None,\n        };\n\n        repo.insert(event.clone(), None).await?;\n\n        // Act\n        OutboxProcessor::drain_batch(&repo, Arc::new(publisher.clone()), 10).await?;\n\n        // Assert\n        let unpublished = repo.fetch_unpublished(10).await?;\n        assert!(unpublished.is_empty(), \"event should be marked as published\");\n\n        let hits = *publisher.published.lock().await;\n        assert_eq!(hits, 1, \"event should have been published exactly once\");\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```",

End-to-End Example\nThe following single file demonstrates a _production-grade_, slice-through implementation\nshowing how EduPulse Live stitches together:\n\n* Service-layer + Repository pattern\n* Domain event publishing\n* JWT-based authentication middleware\n* Redis-backed session management\n* Search indexing (fire-and-forget)\n* TLS configuration\n\n```rust\n//! src/main.rs\n//! In production, design rich error types (crate `thiserror`).\n\nuse std::{net::TcpListener, sync::Arc, time::Duration};\n\nuse actix_session::{config::PersistentSession, storage::RedisSessionStore, tokio::{signal, task};\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\n// ---------- Domain Model ----------------------------------------------------\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize, Clone)]\npub struct LearningPulse Authentication --------------------------------------------------\n\nconst JWT_EXPIRY_SECS: u64 = 60 * 60 * 2; // 2 hours\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\nstruct Claims {\n    sub: String, // user id\n    exp: usize,\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct JwtKeys {\n    enc: EncodingKey,\n    dec: DecodingKey,\n}\n\nimpl JwtKeys {\n    pub fn new(secret: &[u8]) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            enc: EncodingKey::from_secret(secret),\n            dec: DecodingKey::from_secret(secret),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\npub fn generate_jwt(user_id: Uuid, keys: &JwtKeys) -> Result<String> {\n    let claims = Claims {\n        sub: user_id.to_string(),\n        exp: (Utc::now().timestamp() as u64 + JWT_EXPIRY_SECS) as usize,\n    };\n    encode(&Header::default(), &claims, &keys.enc).context(\"sign jwt\")\n}\n\npub fn validate_jwt(token: &str, keys: &JwtKeys) -> Result<Uuid> {\n    let data = decode::<Claims>(\n        token,\n        &keys.dec,\n        &Validation::new(Algorithm::HS256),\n    )\n    .context(\"decode jwt\")?;\n    Ok(Uuid::parse_str(&data.claims.sub)?)\n}\n\n// ---------- Domain Events ---------------------------------------------------\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum DomainEvent {\n    PulseCreated { pulse_id: Uuid, teacher_id: Uuid },\n    // \u2026 more RedisEventPublisher {\n    conn: ConnectionManager,\n}\n\nimpl RedisEventPublisher {\n    pub async fn new(redis_uri: &str) -> Result<Self> {\n        let client = redis::Client::open(redis_uri)?;\n        let conn = ConnectionManager::new(client).await?;\n        Ok(Self { conn })\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl EventPublisher for RedisEventPublisher {\n    async fn publish(&self, event: DomainEvent) -> Result<()> {\n        let payload = serde_json::to_string(&event)?;\n        let _: () = self\n            .conn\n            .clone()\n            .xadd(\"edupulse_events\", \"*\", &[(\"event\", &payload)])\n            .await?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n// ---------- Repository Layer ------------------------------------------------\n\n#[async_trait]\npub trait PgPulseRepository {\n    async fn create(&self, pulse: &LearningPulse) -> Result<()> {\n        sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            INSERT INTO learning_pulses (id, teacher_id, title, description, created_at)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)\n            \"#,\n            pulse.id,\n            pulse.teacher_id,\n            pulse.title,\n            pulse.description,\n            pulse.created_at\n        )\n        .execute(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn list_by_teacher(&self, teacher: Uuid) -> Result<Vec<LearningPulse>> {\n tests).\n#[async_trait]\npub trait OutboxRepository {\n    async fn insert(\n        &self,\n        tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n        envelope: &EventEnvelope,\n    ) -> Result<(),        return Ok(());\n        }\n        let ids: Vec<Uuid> = envelopes.iter().map(|e| e.id).collect();\n        sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            UPDATE event_outbox\n            SET coordinates persistence and dispatching.\npub struct OutboxService<R: OutboxRepository + Send + Sync> {\n    repo:        Arc<R>,\n    nats_url:    String,\n    key_pair:    Arc<Ed25519KeyPair>,\n    // Retry/backoff configuration.\n    max_batch:   i64,\n    poll_every:  Duration,\n}\n\nimpl<R: OutboxRepository + Send + Sync> OutboxService<R> {\n    pub fn new(\n        repo: Arc<R>,\n *synchronous* with respect to the caller\u2019s DB\n    /// transaction; the actual dispatch happens in the background\n    /// daemon spawned by `run_dispatch_loop`.\n    pub async fn stage_event<E: };\n\n        unsigned.signature = self.sign_payload(&unsigned)?;\n\n        self.repo.insert(tx, &unsigned).await\n    }\n\n    /// Infinite loop: regularly pulls unsent events and publishes them.\n    ///\n    /// Should be run in its own Tokio task; gracefully stops when the\n    /// task is cancelled.\n    pub async fn run_dispatch_loop(self: Arc<Self>) -> Result<(), OutboxError> {\n        let nats_conn = async_nats::connect(self.nats_url.clone()).await?;\n\n        loop {\n            // Fetch up to `max_batch` events that still need sending.\n            let events = self.repo.fetch_unsent(self.max_batch).await?;\n\n            if events.is_empty() {\n                sleep(self.poll_every).await;\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // We use a `FuturesUnordered` stream to publish in parallel\n            // while still limiting overall memory / network utilisation.\n            let publish_fut = stream::iter(events.clone())\n                .map(|evt| {\n                    let conn = &nats_conn;\n                    async move {\n                        conn.publish(evt.subject(), serde_json::to_vec(&evt)?)\n                            .await\n                            .map_err(OutboxError::from)\n                    }\n                })\n                .buffer_unordered(16)\n                .collect::<Vec<_>>();\n\n            let results = publish_fut.await;\n\n            // Separate errors from successes for partial retries.\n            let (oks, errs): (Vec<_>, Vec<_>) =\n                results.into_iter().partition(Result::is_ok);\n\n            if !oks.is_empty() {\n                // Only mark events sent when the publish actually succeeded.\n                let sent_events: Vec<_> = events\n                    .iter()\n                    .zip(oks)\n                    .filter_map(|(evt, res)| res.ok().map(|_| evt.clone()))\n                    .collect();\n\n                self.repo.mark_sent(&sent_events).await?;\n            }\n\n            if !errs.is_empty() {\n                // Log and backoff; caller decides global error handling.\n                tracing::warn!(\n                    failed = errs.len(),\n                    \"Some messages failed to publish; will retry\"\n                );\n                // Exponential-ish backoff for noisy neighbours.\n                sleep(self.poll_every * 2).await;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn sign_payload(&self, envelope: &EventEnvelope) -> Result<String, OutboxError> {\n        let mut bytes = serde_json::to_vec(envelope)\n            .map_err(|e| OutboxError::Other(format!(\"serde: {e}\")))?;\n\n        // Sign the raw bytes (comment this if you prefer canonical JSON).\n        let sig = self.key_pair.sign(&mut bytes);\n        Ok(base64::encode(sig.as_ref()))\n    }\n}\n\n/// Example domain event.\n///\n/// In real code these live inside domain modules; kept here for demo.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct LessonPublished {\n    pub lesson_id: Uuid,\n    pub title:     String,\n    pub author_id: Uuid,\n    pub tags:      Vec<String>,\n}\n\nimpl DomainEvent for LessonPublished {\n    fn event_type(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"lesson.published.v1\"\n    }\n}\n\n/// Convenience helper for crafting an Ed25519 key pair from disk/env.\n///\n/// In production you would keep the private key in Hashicorp Vault\n/// or a TPM; this simplistic helper is for local development only.\npub fn load_signing_key() -> Result<Ed25519KeyPair, OutboxError> {\n    use ring::rand::SystemRandom;\n    use ring::signature::Ed25519KeyPair as Key;\n\n    if let Ok(pkcs8_b64) = std::env::var(\"EDUPULSE_SIGNING_KEY_B64\") {\n        let bytes = base64::decode(pkcs8_b64)\n            .map_err(|_| OutboxError::Crypto)?;\n        Key::from_pkcs8(&bytes).map_err(|_| OutboxError::Crypto)\n    } else {\n        // Auto-generate volatile key when none provided.\n        let rng = SystemRandom::new();\n        let pkcs8 = Key::generate_pkcs8(&rng).map_err(|_| OutboxError::Crypto)?;\n        Ok(Key::from_pkcs8(pkcs8.as_ref()).map_err(|_| OutboxError::Crypto)?)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Bootstraps a producer demo.\n///\n/// This async function illustrates how to embed the Outbox transaction\n/// into domain service logic.  Remove or adjust for production usage.\npub async fn demo_produce_event(db_url: &str) -> Result<(), OutboxError> {\n    let pool = PgPoolOptions::new()\n        .max_connections(5)\n        .connect(db_url)\n        .await?;\n\n    let repo = Arc::new(PgOutboxRepository::new(pool.clone()));\n    let key_pair = load_signing_key()?;\n    let outbox = Arc::new(OutboxService::new(\n        repo.clone(),\n        \"tls://connect.ngs.global\".to_string(),\n        key_pair,\n    ));\n\n    // spawn the background dispatcher\n    tokio::spawn(outbox.clone().run_dispatch_loop());\n\n    // Business transaction: create lesson, persist event, commit.\n    let mut tx = pool.begin().await?;\n\n    // Imagine we create a lesson in lessons table here \u2026\n\n    let event = LessonPublished {\n        lesson_id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n        title:     \"Algebraic Topology 101\".to_owned(),\n        author_id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n        tags:      vec![\"math\".into(), \"topology\".into()],\n    };\n\n    outbox\n        .stage_event(&mut tx, event.lesson_id, &event)\n        .await?;\n\n    tx.commit().await?;\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n```",

It follows the Service-Layer + Repository pattern,\n//! emits domain events, and is fully asynchronous.\n//!\n//! The implementation intentionally avoids leaking concrete I/O details\n//! to ease unit testing\u2014external concerns (SQL database, message broker)\n//! are injected behind traits.\n//!\n//! Dependencies (add to Cargo.toml if missing):\n//!   async-trait    = \"0.1\"\n//!   chrono         = { version = \"0.4\", features = [\"serde\"] }\n//!   serde          = { version = \"1\", features = [\"derive\"] }\n//!   sqlx           = { version = \"0.7\", default-features = false, features = [\"rustls\",\"postgres\",\"macros\",\"chrono\"] }\n//!   thiserror      = \"1\"\n//!\n//! The rest of the crate is expected to provide real implementations of\n//! `EventPublisher` and `PgPool`.\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse sqlx::{postgres::PgRow, PgPool, Row};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\n/// Domain object representing a learning pulse (challenge/activity).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct LearningPulse {\n    pub id: Uuid,\n    pub author_id: Uuid,\n    pub title: String,\n    pub body: String,\n    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub due_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    pub is_archived: bool,\n}\n\n/// Domain object for a student response to a pulse.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct PulseResponse {\n    pub id: Uuid,\n    pub pulse_id: Uuid,\n    pub responder_id: Uuid,\n    pub content_uri: String,\n    pub submitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/// Events the module can publish downstream.\n///\n/// NOTE: Versioned event naming scheme, e.g. `PulseCreated.v1`,\n/// guarantees forward compatibility when the payload shape changes.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(tag = \"type\", content = \"data\")]\npub enum PulseEvent {\n    #[serde(rename = \"PulseCreated.v1\")]\n    PulseCreated {\n        pulse_id: Uuid,\n        author_id: Uuid,\n        title: String,\n    },\n    #[serde(rename = \"PulseResponded.v1\")]\n    PulseResponded {\n        pulse_id: Uuid,\n        responder_id: Uuid,\n        response_id: Uuid,\n        content_uri: String,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Injectable message publisher for decoupling side-effects.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait EventPublisher: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn publish(&self, event: PulseEvent) -> Result<(), PublishError>;\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum PublishError {\n    #[error(\"broker disconnected\")]\n    Disconnected,\n    #[error(\"serialization error: {0}\")]\n    Serialization(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n    #[error(\"unknown publish error: {0}\")]\n    Other(String),\n}\n\n/// Persistence layer errors.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum RepositoryError {\n    #[error(\"entity not found\")]\n    NotFound,\n    #[error(\"database error: {0}\")]\n    Db(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n}\n\n/// Service-level error enumeration.\n///\n/// Explicit conversion From<RepositoryError> is implemented so\n/// caller code can use `?` without additional noise.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum PulseServiceError {\n    #[error(\"input validation failed: {0}\")]\n    Validation(String),\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Repository(#[from] RepositoryError),\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Publisher(#[from] PublishError),\n}\n\n/// Repository abstraction for learning pulses.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait PulseRepository: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn insert(&self, pulse: &LearningPulse) -> Result<(), RepositoryError>;\n    async fn find(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<LearningPulse, RepositoryError>;\n    async fn archive(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<(), RepositoryError>;\n}\n\n/// Repository abstraction for pulse responses.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait ResponseRepository: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn insert(&self, resp: &PulseResponse) -> Result<(), RepositoryError>;\n    async fn list_for_pulse(&self, pulse_id: Uuid) -> Result<Vec<PulseResponse>, RepositoryError>;\n}\n\n/// Concrete Postgres implementation of `PulseRepository`.\npub struct PgPulseRepository {\n    pool: PgPool,\n}\n\nimpl PgPulseRepository {\n    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {\n        Self { pool }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl PulseRepository for PgPulseRepository {\n    async fn insert(&self, pulse: &LearningPulse) -> Result<(), RepositoryError> {\n        sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            INSERT INTO learning_pulses (id, author_id, title, body, created_at, due_at, is_archived)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7)\n            \"#,\n            pulse.id,\n            pulse.author_id,\n            pulse.title,\n            pulse.body,\n            pulse.created_at,\n            pulse.due_at,\n            pulse.is_archived\n        )\n        .execute(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn find(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<LearningPulse, RepositoryError> {\n        let row: PgRow = sqlx::query(\n            r#\"\n            SELECT id, author_id, title, body, created_at, due_at, is_archived\n            FROM learning_pulses\n            WHERE id = $1\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .bind(id)\n        .fetch_one(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(LearningPulse {\n            id: row.get(\"id\"),\n            author_id: row.get(\"author_id\"),\n            title: row.get(\"title\"),\n            body: row.get(\"body\"),\n            created_at: row.get(\"created_at\"),\n            due_at: row.try_get(\"due_at\")?,\n            is_archived: row.get(\"is_archived\"),\n        })\n    }\n\n    async fn archive(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<(), RepositoryError> {\n        let res = sqlx::query!(\n            \"UPDATE learning_pulses SET is_archived = TRUE WHERE id = $1\",\n            id\n        )\n        .execute(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n\n        if res.rows_affected() == 0 {\n            Err(RepositoryError::NotFound)\n        } else {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Concrete Postgres implementation of `ResponseRepository`.\npub struct PgResponseRepository {\n    pool: PgPool,\n}\n\nimpl PgResponseRepository {\n    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {\n        Self { pool }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl ResponseRepository for PgResponseRepository {\n    async fn insert(&self, resp: &PulseResponse) -> Result<(), RepositoryError> {\n        sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            INSERT INTO pulse_responses (id, pulse_id, responder_id, content_uri, submitted_at)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)\n            \"#,\n            resp.id,\n            resp.pulse_id,\n            resp.responder_id,\n            resp.content_uri,\n            resp.submitted_at\n        )\n        .execute(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn list_for_pulse(&self, pulse_id: Uuid) -> Result<Vec<PulseResponse>, RepositoryError> {\n        let rows = sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"\n            SELECT id, pulse_id, responder_id, content_uri, submitted_at\n            FROM pulse_responses\n            WHERE pulse_id = $1\n            \"#,\n            pulse_id\n        )\n        .fetch_all(&self.pool)\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(rows\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|r| PulseResponse {\n                id: r.id,\n                pulse_id: r.pulse_id,\n                responder_id: r.responder_id,\n                content_uri: r.content_uri,\n                submitted_at: r.submitted_at,\n            })\n            .collect())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Service facade\u2014entry point used by controllers / GraphQL resolvers.\npub struct PulseService<R: PulseRepository, S: ResponseRepository, P: EventPublisher> {\n    pulses: R,\n    responses: S,\n    publisher: P,\n}\n\nimpl<R: PulseRepository, S: ResponseRepository, P: EventPublisher> PulseService<R, S, P> {\n    pub fn new(pulses: R, responses: S, publisher: P) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            pulses,\n            responses,\n            publisher,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Creates a new learning pulse and publishes `PulseCreated` event.\n    pub async fn create_pulse(\n        &self,\n        author_id: Uuid,\n        title: &str,\n        body: &str,\n        due_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    ) -> Result<LearningPulse, PulseServiceError> {\n        if title.trim().is_empty() {\n            return Err(PulseServiceError::Validation(\n                \"title must not be empty\".into(),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        let pulse = LearningPulse {\n            id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n            author_id,\n            title: title.trim().to_owned(),\n            body: body.to_owned(),\n            created_at: Utc::now(),\n            due_at,\n            is_archived: false,\n        };\n\n        self.pulses.insert(&pulse).await?;\n\n        // Fire-and-forget the event; let caller decide whether to await or spawn.\n        self.publisher\n            .publish(PulseEvent::PulseCreated {\n                pulse_id: pulse.id,\n                author_id: pulse.author_id,\n                title: pulse.title.clone(),\n            })\n            .await?;\n\n        Ok(pulse)\n    }\n\n    /// Adds a student response to a pulse and publishes `PulseResponded`.\n    pub async fn respond_to_pulse(\n        &self,\n        pulse_id: Uuid,\n        responder_id: Uuid,\n        content_uri: &str,\n    ) -> Result<PulseResponse, PulseServiceError> {\n        // Validate pulse existence.\n        let pulse = self.pulses.find(pulse_id).await?;\n        if pulse.is_archived {\n            return Err(PulseServiceError::Validation(\n                \"Cannot respond to an archived pulse\".into(),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        if content_uri.trim().is_empty() {\n            return Err(PulseServiceError::Validation(\n                \"content_uri must not be empty\".into(),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        let resp = PulseResponse {\n            id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n            pulse_id,\n            responder_id,\n            content_uri: content_uri.trim().to_owned(),\n            submitted_at: Utc::now(),\n        };\n\n        self.responses.insert(&resp).await?;\n\n        self.publisher\n            .publish(PulseEvent::PulseResponded {\n                pulse_id,\n                responder_id,\n                response_id: resp.id,\n                content_uri: resp.content_uri.clone(),\n            })\n            .await?;\n\n        Ok(resp)\n    }\n\n    /// Returns all responses for a given pulse.\n    pub async fn list_responses(\n        &self,\n        pulse_id: Uuid,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<PulseResponse>, PulseServiceError> {\n        Ok(self.responses.list_for_pulse(pulse_id).await?)\n    }\n\n    /// Archives a learning pulse (soft-delete).\n    pub async fn archive_pulse(&self, pulse_id: Uuid) -> Result<(), PulseServiceError> {\n        self.pulses.archive(pulse_id).await?;\n        // Future: publish `PulseArchived` event here\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------\n .ok_or(RepositoryError::NotFound)\n        }\n\n        async fn archive(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<(), RepositoryError> {\n            let mut guard = self.0.lock().unwrap();\n            let p =
